				tradername: 'yw_app',
				trader: "pc",
				closesignature: "yes",
				signature_method: "md5",
				timestamp:new Date().getTime(), //new Date().getTime()
				signature: "****",
				token:gltoken
			}

				type:"post",
				url:url,
				data:params,
				async:true,
				success:function(data){

                                                if(data.data.is_expire==0){//未过期

				jQuery.cookie("is_vip", 1, {path: '/',domain: '.111.com.cn'})
			}else if(data.data.is_expire==1){//过期
				jQuery.cookie("is_vip", -1, {path: '/',domain: '.111.com.cn'})
				jQuery("#logininfo img").remove();
			}

                                                 jQuery.cookie("is_vip",0,{path:'/', domain: '.111.com.cn'});

					}
                                   }
				}
			});
	}

function topAds(picArr,obj){
    if(picArr[0]['adList'].length > 0){                                                                
        var zhref = picArr [0]['adList'][0].picturelink;
        var sname = picArr[0]['adList'][0].tishi;
        var sksrc = picArr[0]['adList'][0].pictureurlbig;
        var szsrc = picArr[0]['adList'][0].pictureurl;
		var _height = picArr[0]['adList'].height;
        var $links = jQuery('link');//用于其它非首页判断宽窄屏
        for(var j=0;j<$links.length;j++){
            if($links.eq(j).attr('href').indexOf('head_990') > -1){
                isWidescreen = false;//窄
                break;
            }else{
                isWidescreen = true;//宽
            }
        }
        if(sksrc==" "&&szsrc==" "){
            sksrc=null;
            zxsrc=null;
        }
        var isWidescreen=jQuery('.site-nav-bd').width()>=1190;
        var isIndex = window.location.href.indexOf("www.111.com.cn/product") != -1;
        var isAllCatalog = window.location.href.indexOf("www.111.com.cn/categories") != -1;
        if(isWidescreen && !isIndex && !isAllCatalog){
             jQuery('#topCurtain').css('width','1190px');
             jQuery(obj).attr({
                "href":zhref,
                "title":sname
            });
            jQuery(obj).find("img").attr({
                "id":"toptrack",
                "src":sksrc,
                "width":1190,
                "height":_height
            });                                                     
        }else{
           jQuery('#topCurtain').css('width','990px');
           jQuery(obj).attr({
                "href":zhref,
                "title":sname
            });
            jQuery(obj).find("img").attr({
                "id":"toptrack",
                "src":szsrc,
                "width":990,
                "height":_height
            });
        }
        //jQuery('#topCurtain').show();
    }else{
        jQuery('#topCurtain').remove();
    }
}

function gotoMyPrivateCustom(){
	if(jQuery("meta[name='index']").length < 1){
		jQuery.cookie("privateCustomLogin", true, {path:'/', domain: '.111.com.cn'});
		window.location.href = '//www.111.com.cn';
		return;
	}
	if(createUser()){
		window.location.href = '//my.111.com.cn/ucenter/privateTag.action';
	} else {
		showPrivateCustom();
	}
}

    function getQueryString(name) {
            var reg = new RegExp("(^|&)" + name + "=([^&]*)(&|$)", "i");
            var r = window.location.search.substr(1).match(reg);
            if (r != null) return unescape(r[2]); return null;
        }
        try {

jQuery('#browseDiv li a').each(function(){this.href+=((this.href.indexOf('?')>1?'&':'?')+'siteid=4');});

            var uuid = (jQuery.cookie('UUID'));
            var UserId = jQuery.cookie('JUD')||"";

    if(typeof window.localStorage !== 'undefined'&&tu*1!=1){
        
                sessionStorage.setItem("tracker_u",tu);
                localStorage.setItem("tracker_u",tu);
                 }
             }
             if(tu==null&&tracker_u==null&&referrer==''){
                 jQuery.cookie('tracker_u', 1000000, {path: '/', domain: '.111.com.cn', expires: 1});
    if(typeof window.localStorage !== 'undefined'&&tu*1!=1){
        
                sessionStorage.setItem("tracker_u",1000000);
                localStorage.setItem("tracker_u",1000000);
                 }
             }
             if(tu==null&&tracker_u==null&&referrer!=''){
                  tu='';
                  if(referrer.indexOf("baidu")>-1){
                           tu=2000000;
                  }
                  else if(referrer.indexOf("haosou")>-1){
                           tu=2000001;
                  }
                 else if(referrer.indexOf("sogou")>-1){
                           tu=2000002;
                  }
                  else if(referrer.indexOf("soso")>-1){
                           tu=2000003;
                  }
                 else if(referrer.indexOf("bing")>-1){
                           tu=2000004;
                  } else if(referrer.indexOf("111.com.cn")<=-1){
                           tu=3000000;
                   }
                  if(tu!=''){
                      jQuery.cookie('tracker_u', tu, {path: '/', domain: '.111.com.cn', expires: 1});
                  }

             }

            if(visitid == null) {
                visitid = Math.uuid();
                jQuery.cookie('visitid', visitid, {path: '/', domain: '.111.com.cn', expires: 1/48});
            }
            if (uuid == null) {
                uuid = Math.uuid();
                jQuery.cookie('UUID', uuid, {path: '/', domain: '.111.com.cn', expires: 1});
            }
            tracker_u=(jQuery.cookie('tracker_u'));
            var cururl = document.location.href;
            cururl = cururl.replace(/&/g, '~@~')
            referrer = referrer.replace(/&/g, '~@~')
            var str = "uuid=" + uuid + "&action=none&autumn=offical&userid=" + UserId + "&refer=" + referrer + "&cururl=" + cururl+"&tracker_u="+tracker_u+"&visitid="+visitid;

            var url = "//nest.111.com.cn?" + str;
            jQuery.ajax({ type: "get", url: url, async: true, dataType: 'jsonp',
                jsonpCallback: "cb"
            });

		}
	}

function showFn(id){
     var tag = $("#"+id);
     var proObj = tag.children(".showPro");
     tag.children("ul").find("li").each(function() {
			var htmlObj = $(proObj).children(".f_prod:eq(0)");
			if (htmlObj && htmlObj != null && $(htmlObj).html()) {
                                $(this).append("<div class='f_prod'>"+ $(htmlObj).html()+ "</div>");
	                        $(htmlObj).remove();
		      }
		});
      $(proObj ).remove();
}
